Response PlayerNiceShotBiker
{
	scene "scenes/Biker/NiceShot08.vcd" odds 20 //Good shot. [laughing]

	scene "scenes/Biker/C6DLC3FIRSTSAFEROOM02.vcd" //Whoa. How'd you do that?
	scene "scenes/Biker/ViolenceAwe06.vcd"  //Did u see that?
	scene "scenes/Biker/Worldairport0322.vcd"  //Hehe...hot shot!
}

	Response PlayerNiceShotBiker
}

Response SurvivorMournBillBiker
{
	scene "scenes/Biker/C6DLC3BILLDIES01.vcd" then Manager ConceptBlock017 foo:0 0 //Bill! It should have been Louis! It should have been Louis!
	scene "scenes/Biker/C6DLC3BILLDIES06.vcd" odds 10 //Thanks Bill, I owe you one. You old bastard...
	scene "scenes/Biker/C6DLC3ZOEYDIES01.vcd" then Manager InfoRemc7m1_pretank02 foo:0 0 //Noooo! You monsters! Take Louis instead!
	scene "scenes/Biker/GoingToDieLight16.vcd"  //Killed by vampires. What a goddamn disgrace.
}
Rule SurvivorMournBillBiker
{
	criteria ConceptPlayerSeeDeadPlayer IsBiker IsDeadNamvet IsNotSaidSomeoneDied IsTalk IsTalkBiker IsWorldTalkBiker
	Response SurvivorMournBillBiker
}

{

	scene "scenes/Biker/Thanks08.vcd" predelay ".2,.5" then Subject PlayerYouAreWelcome foo:0 0 //Thank you.
	scene "scenes/Biker/Thanks09.vcd" predelay ".2,.5" then Subject PlayerYouAreWelcome foo:0 0 //Thanks, I owe ya.
	scene "scenes/Biker/Thanks11.vcd" predelay ".2,.5" then Subject PlayerYouAreWelcome foo:0 0 //Thanks, dude.
	scene "scenes/Biker/Thanks12.vcd" predelay ".2,.5" then Subject PlayerYouAreWelcome foo:0 0 //Thanks for that.
	scene "scenes/Biker/Thanks13.vcd" predelay ".2,.5" then Subject PlayerYouAreWelcome foo:0 0 //Thanks bro.
	scene "scenes/Biker/Thanks14.vcd" predelay ".2,.5" then Subject PlayerYouAreWelcome foo:0 0 //Thanks brother.
	scene "scenes/Biker/ToTheRescueThanks03.vcd" predelay ".2,.5" then Subject PlayerYouAreWelcome foo:0 0 //Hey, thanks for not forgettin' me.
	scene "scenes/Biker/ToTheRescueThanks05.vcd" predelay ".2,.5" then Subject PlayerYouAreWelcome foo:0 0 //Hell, I guess that's one I owe YOU.
	scene "scenes/Biker/Thanks06.vcd" predelay ".2,.5" then Subject PlayerYouAreWelcome foo:0 0 //Hey, thanks man.
}
Rule ThanksGotItemBiker
{
	criteria IsAwardConcept IsSharingSubject SubjectIsBiker IsTalk IsTalkBiker
	Response ThanksGotItemBiker
}

//--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Response PlayerCallForRescueBiker
{
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue01" noscene //I could use some help over here! Anyone?
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue02" noscene //Anyone out there?  I got myself stuck in here!
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue03" noscene odds 10 //Get me the hell out of here!
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue04" noscene //Heeeeyyyy! Can anyone here me?  I could use a hand.
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue06" noscene //Goddammit, I'm stuck in here!  Someone let me out!
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue07" noscene //When you get a chance, can you guys get me outta here?
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue08" noscene //If it ain't too much trouble, I could use a hand out of here!
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue09" noscene //Hey, can anyone hear me?  I got my ass stuck in here.
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue10" noscene odds 10 //Someone want to let me outta here?
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue11" noscene //Ah shit I'm stuck! C'mon! I could use a hand out of here!
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue12" noscene //[Grunting]  Shit, I'm stuck in here!  Someone give me a hand!
	speak "Player.Biker_CallForRescue13" noscene odds 10 //Goddamn it!  I need to get the hell out of here!
	speak "Player.Biker_LostCall01" noscene odds 10 //Hello
	speak "Player.Biker_LostCall04" noscene odds 10 //Is anyone there?
	speak "Player.Biker_LostCall05" noscene //Marco!
	speak "Player.Biker_LostCall08" noscene odds 10 //Hello? Where dija go?
}
Rule PlayerCallForRescueBiker
{
	criteria ConceptCallForRescue IsBiker IsTalk IsTalkBiker IsWorldTalkBiker
	Response PlayerCallForRescueBiker
}
